## Cloud Monitoring

This category covers monitoring solutions for various cloud platforms, including Azure, AWS, and Google Cloud. It is essential for ensuring the performance and reliability of applications running in cloud environments.

**Stats**: 3 modules • 330 pages • 3.0 hours • intermediate

### Monitoring Azure Services with Dynatrace

This module covers the setup and monitoring of various Microsoft Azure services using Dynatrace, including full-stack, infrastructure, and log monitoring capabilities.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.75
- Pages: 138

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of Microsoft Azure services
- Familiarity with Dynatrace monitoring concepts
- Intermediate knowledge of cloud service metrics

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Configure Dynatrace for monitoring Microsoft Azure environments
- Integrate Dynatrace with various Azure services
- Monitor specific Azure services like App Service and Azure AI components
- View and analyze service metrics in the Dynatrace environment

### AWS Monitoring with Dynatrace

This module provides comprehensive guidance on monitoring various AWS services using Dynatrace, including setup, integration, and troubleshooting techniques.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 10.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.74
- Pages: 125

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of AWS services
- Familiarity with Dynatrace platform
- Knowledge of cloud monitoring concepts

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Understand how to set up Dynatrace for monitoring AWS services
- Integrate OneAgent with different AWS services for full-stack observability
- Configure monitoring for serverless applications and troubleshoot integration issues

## Log Monitoring

This category focuses on the essentials of log monitoring, providing insights into application performance and troubleshooting. It is crucial for identifying issues and maintaining application health.

**Stats**: 2 modules • 171 pages • 2.0 hours • intermediate

### Log Monitoring Essentials

This module covers the comprehensive aspects of log monitoring within the Dynatrace platform, including log ingestion, processing, and analysis from various sources.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.66
- Pages: 110

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of log management concepts.
- Familiarity with the Dynatrace platform and its interface.
- Knowledge of cloud environments and log data sources.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Understand how to configure automatic log collection and processing in Dynatrace.
- Set up and manage log sources and storage configurations.
- Implement log forwarding from cloud providers to Dynatrace.
- Utilize the Log Ingestion API for streaming log records.
- Enhance log data with automatic enrichment features.
- Configure log ingest rules and rotation patterns for effective monitoring.

- [Management zones and ingested log data (Logs Classic) — Dynatrace Docs](https://docs.dynatrace.com/docs/analyze-explore-automate/log-monitoring/analyze-log-data/management-zones-and-log-monitoring) (concept)

### Kubernetes Log Management with Dynatrace

This module covers the deployment and configuration of log collection and monitoring in Kubernetes environments using Dynatrace, Fluent Bit, and Fluentd.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 6.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.68
- Pages: 61

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic knowledge of Kubernetes architecture
- Familiarity with Dynatrace platform
- Understanding of logging concepts and tools

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Configure Fluent Bit and Fluentd for log collection in Kubernetes
- Implement log ingestion rules for effective log management
- Understand the differences between Classic and Grail metrics
- Predict and autoscale Kubernetes workloads using Dynatrace

## OneAgent Configuration

This category provides guidance on configuring and monitoring with OneAgent, a key component of Dynatrace. Proper configuration is vital for accurate performance monitoring.

**Stats**: 2 modules • 106 pages • 2.0 hours • intermediate

### OneAgent Monitoring and Configuration

This module covers the comprehensive functionalities, deployment, and configuration of OneAgent within Dynatrace, including log ingestion, monitoring capabilities, and API integrations.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.66
- Pages: 91

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of application performance monitoring concepts.
- Familiarity with Dynatrace platform and its components.
- Knowledge of API usage and configuration management.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Understand how OneAgent operates and its role in performance monitoring.
- Configure log ingestion and manage custom log sources using OneAgent.
- Utilize the Dynatrace API to manage OneAgent configurations and retrieve monitoring data.
- Deploy OneAgent in various environments, including AWS and container services.

### DQL Commands Overview

This module covers the essential commands and functionalities of Dynatrace Query Language (DQL) for effective data querying and log processing within Dynatrace.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.61
- Pages: 54

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of log management concepts
- Familiarity with data querying principles
- Experience with Dynatrace UI

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Implement DQL matchers to filter log data effectively
- Convert log matching rules from LQL to DQL
- Apply filter syntax to create effective filter statements in Dynatrace
- Understand the structure and components of Dynatrace Pattern Language
- Extract fields from records using DPL Architect
- Identify and explain the purpose of DPL Positional Matchers in log processing
- Identify and match UUIDs within text strings
- Understand how to use DQL Aggregation commands to analyze data
- Generate sample data using the data command
- Understand how to use the timeseries command in DQL

- Cohesion: 0.57

- Understand and implement different authentication options for the Dynatrace API.

- Manage configurations for web applications and content resources using the API.
- Handle tenant tokens and application tagging through API calls.

### Dynatrace Authentication APIs

This module covers various APIs related to authentication and data retrieval within the Dynatrace platform, focusing on managing subscription costs, application monitoring, and security threats.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 5.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.57
- Pages: 68

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of RESTful APIs
- Familiarity with JSON data formats
- Knowledge of Dynatrace platform functionalities

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Retrieve cost allocation data for Dynatrace subscriptions.
- Access and manage attack data for application security.
- Utilize entity selectors for efficient API data queries.
- Fetch problem lists and details from the Problems API.
- Identify geographic entities for Real User Monitoring.
- Retrieve inline code and JavaScript tags for application integration.
- Understand and retrieve effective configuration settings.
- List all applications and their parameters in a Dynatrace environment.

### Policy Management API Overview

This module covers the functionalities of the Policy Management API in Dynatrace, including managing policy boundaries and access policies through various API operations.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 3.5 hours
- Cohesion: 0.64
- Pages: 17

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of API concepts and RESTful services.
- Familiarity with Dynatrace platform and its user management features.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- List, view, create, update, and delete policy boundaries and access policies using the Dynatrace API.
- Understand the authentication requirements and response codes for API requests.
- Configure user permissions with fine-granular restrictions using policy boundaries.

### Events API Overview and Migration

This module provides comprehensive documentation on the Events API, including migration from version 1 to version 2, detailed usage of the API for event management, and integration of business events into Dynatrace.

### User Action Properties Guide

This module provides comprehensive guidance on defining, capturing, and leveraging user action and session properties across various application types in Dynatrace, aimed at enhancing user experience and performance analytics.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.65
- Pages: 59

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of Dynatrace functionalities.
- Familiarity with application performance monitoring concepts.
- Knowledge of user experience metrics and analytics.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Identify and troubleshoot common sign-in issues with Dynatrace accounts.
- Extend user experience and behavior data for improved digital monitoring.
- Configure key user actions and session properties for custom and mobile applications.
- Utilize session segmentation for effective customer support.
- Capture event and session properties for both mobile and web frontends.

**Pages:**
- [Session segmentation — Dynatrace Docs](https://docs.dynatrace.com/docs/observe/digital-experience/session-segmentation) (concept)
- [Session Replay — Dynatrace Docs](https://docs.dynatrace.com/docs/observe/digital-experience/session-replay) (concept)
- [User action metrics — Dynatrace Docs](https://docs.dynatrace.com/docs/observe/digital-experience/rum-concepts/user-action-metrics) (concept)

### OpenTelemetry Integration with Dynatrace

This module provides a comprehensive guide on integrating OpenTelemetry with Dynatrace for monitoring various serverless environments, including AWS Lambda, Google Cloud Functions, and Azure Functions, using multiple programming languages.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 8.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.68
- Pages: 48

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of OpenTelemetry concepts.
- Familiarity with Dynatrace monitoring capabilities.
- Experience with serverless architectures and relevant programming languages (e.g., .NET, Java, Node.js, Python).

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Implement OpenTelemetry tracing in .NET, Java, Node.js, and Python for AWS Lambda functions.
- Configure OpenTelemetry interoperability with Dynatrace for unsupported technologies.
- Enable and configure the OpenTelemetry Span Sensor for effective data capture.
- Extend traces and manage spans for improved application monitoring.

### Dynatrace Operator Migration Guide

This module covers the migration processes for various versions of the Dynatrace Operator and DynaKube, including auto-update setup and API transitions.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 4.5 hours
- Cohesion: 0.67
- Pages: 34

**Prerequisites:**
- Familiarity with Kubernetes and Dynatrace Operator.
- Basic understanding of API versioning and migration concepts.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Understand the differences between DynaKube API versions.
- Implement migration processes for DynaKube from v1beta1 to v1beta5.
- Set up auto-updates for the Dynatrace Operator using GitOps.

## Workflows and Automation

- Difficulty: intermediate

- Configure and manage workflows to automate responses to monitoring data.

## Cluster Management

This category covers the management of clusters and high availability within Dynatrace. Proper cluster management is essential for ensuring system reliability and performance.

**Stats**: 1 modules • 11 pages • 1.0 hours • intermediate

### Cluster Management and High Availability

This module covers the essential practices for managing Dynatrace Managed clusters, focusing on high availability, disaster recovery, and data management strategies.

**Metadata:**
- Difficulty: intermediate
- Estimated Time: 6.0 hours
- Cohesion: 0.64
- Pages: 11

**Prerequisites:**
- Basic understanding of Dynatrace Managed architecture.
- Familiarity with data center operations and backup strategies.

**Learning Outcomes:**
- Implement data center disaster recovery from backup and inter-data center recovery using Premium HA.
- Configure rack-aware replication and conversion for optimal data distribution.
- Estimate backup sizes for effective cluster management.
- Perform node operations including start, stop, and restart procedures.
- Understand the functionality of Premium HA in multi-data center environments.
